<script>
function scrollToFrame(id, btn) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.fpage').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) {
    const y = el.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.scrollY - 68;
    window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
  }
}
const frames = ['f1','f2','f3','f4','f5','fc'];
const btns = document.querySelectorAll('.fpage');
window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
  let active = 0;
  frames.forEach((id,i) => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (el && el.getBoundingClientRect().top < window.innerHeight * 0.55) active = i;
  });
  btns.forEach((b,i) => b.classList.toggle('active', i === active));
});
</script>

<script>
function scrollToFrame(id, btn) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.fpage').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) {
    const y = el.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.scrollY - 80;
    window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
  }
}

// Highlight active frame on scroll
const frames = ['f1','f2'];
const btns = document.querySelectorAll('.fpage');
window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
  let active = 0;
  frames.forEach((id, i) => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (!el) return;
    const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
    if (rect.top < window.innerHeight * 0.5) active = i;
  });
  btns.forEach((b,i) => b.classList.toggle('active', i === active));
});
</script>
</body>

<script>
function scrollToFrame(id, btn) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.fpage').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) {
    const y = el.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.scrollY - 68;
    window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
  }
}

// Highlight active frame on scroll
const frames = ['f1','f2','f3','f4','f5','fc'];
const btns = document.querySelectorAll('.fpage');
window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
  let active = 0;
  frames.forEach((id, i) => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (!el) return;
    const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
    if (rect.top < window.innerHeight * 0.5) active = i;
  });
  btns.forEach((b,i) => b.classList.toggle('active', i === active));
});
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
// Page navigation
function go(id, btn) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.fpage').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) {
    const y = el.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.scrollY - 60;
    window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
  }
}

// Overlay sidebar
function toggleOverlay(id) {
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) el.classList.add('show');
}
function closeOverlay(id, evt) {
  if (evt && evt.target.closest('.overlay-sidebar')) return;
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) el.classList.remove('show');
}

// Active page highlight on scroll
const frameIds = ['f9','f10','f11','f12','f13'];
const btns = document.querySelectorAll('.fpage');
window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
  let active = 0;
  frameIds.forEach((id, i) => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (el && el.getBoundingClientRect().top < window.innerHeight * 0.5) active = i;
  });
  btns.forEach((b, i) => b.classList.toggle('active', i === active));
}, { passive: true });

// Live visitor counter simulation
setInterval(() => {
  const el = document.getElementById('activeV');
  if (el) {
    const v = parseInt(el.textContent) || 84;
    el.textContent = Math.max(50, Math.min(150, v + Math.floor(Math.random() * 7) - 3));
  }
}, 4000);
</script>

<script>
function go(id, btn) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.fpage').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) {
    const y = el.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.scrollY - 68;
    window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
  }
}

const frameIds = ['f1','f2','f3','f4','f5','f6','f7','f8','f9','f10','f11','f12','f13'];
const btns = document.querySelectorAll('.fpage');
window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
  let active = 0;
  frameIds.forEach((id, i) => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (el && el.getBoundingClientRect().top < window.innerHeight * 0.5) active = i;
  });
  btns.forEach((b, i) => b.classList.toggle('active', i === active));
}, { passive: true });
</script>
</body>
</html>

<script>
function go(id, btn) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.fpage').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (el) {
    const y = el.getBoundingClientRect().top + window.scrollY - 68;
    window.scrollTo({ top: y, behavior: 'smooth' });
  }
}

const frameIds = ['fd1','fd2','fd3','fd4','fm1','fm2','fm3','fm4'];
const btns = document.querySelectorAll('.fpage');
window.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
  let active = 0;
  frameIds.forEach((id, i) => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (el && el.getBoundingClientRect().top < window.innerHeight * 0.5) active = i;
  });
  btns.forEach((b, i) => b.classList.toggle('active', i === active));
}, { passive: true });
</script>
</body>
</html>
